\'\';\n        let currentStep = 1;\n\n        // Initialize Socket.IO\n        function initSocket() {\n            socket = io(\'http://localhost:3002\');\n            \n            socket.on(\'connect\', () => {\n                console.log(\'Connected to Murphy System\');\n                showStatus(\'Connected to Murphy System\', 3000);\n            });\n\n            socket.on(\'disconnect\', () => {\n                console.log(\'Disconnected from Murphy System\');\n                showStatus(\'Disconnected - Reconnecting...\', 0);\n            });\n\n            socket.on(\'task_update\', (data) => {\n                console.log(\'Task update:\', data);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Task Update: ${data.message || JSON.stringify(data)}`, \'system\');\n            });\n\n            socket.on(\'error\', (error) => {\n                console.error(\'Socket error:\', error);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Error: ${error.message || error}`, \'system\');\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Onboarding Functions\n        function nextStep(step) {\n            document.getElementById(`step${currentStep}`).classList.remove(\'active\');\n            document.getElementById(`step${step}`).classList.add(\'active\');\n            currentStep = step;\n        }\n\n        async function completeOnboarding() {\n            userName = document.getElementById(\'user-name\').value || \'User\';\n            businessType = document.getElementById(\'business-type\').value || \'General\';\n            userGoal = document.getElementById(\'user-goal\').value || \'Automation\';\n\n            // Hide onboarding\n            document.getElementById(\'onboarding-modal\').style.display = \'none\';\n\n            // Update greeting\n            document.getElementById(\'user-greeting\').textContent = \n                `Welcome ${userName} | ${businessType} | Goal: ${userGoal}`;\n\n            // Initialize system\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/initialize\', {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        user_name: userName,\n                        business_type: businessType,\n                        goal: userGoal\n                    })\n                });\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `System initialized for ${userName}. Ready to assist with ${businessType} automation.`, \'system\');\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Initialization error:\', error);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \'System initialized in offline mode. Some features may be limited.\', \'system\');\n            }\n\n            // Initialize socket\n            initSocket();\n        }\n\n        // Message Functions\n        function addMessage(type, content, cssClass) {\n            const messagesEl = document.getElementById(\'messages\');\n            const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();\n            \n            const messageEl = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            messageEl.className = \'message\';\n            messageEl.innerHTML = `\n                <div class="message-header">\n                    <span class="message-type ${cssClass}">${type}</span>\n                    <span class="message-time">${time}</span>\n                </div>\n                <div class="message-content ${cssClass}">${escapeHtml(content)}</div>\n            `;\n            \n            messagesEl.appendChild(messageEl);\n            \n            // Scroll to bottom\n            messagesEl.scrollTop = messagesEl.scrollHeight;\n        }\n\n        function escapeHtml(text) {\n            const div = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            div.textContent = text;\n            return div.innerHTML;\n        }\n\n        // Input Handling\n        function handleKeyPress(event) {\n            if (event.key === \'Enter\') {\n                handleSubmit();\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function handleSubmit() {\n            const input = document.getElementById(\'user-input\');\n            const message = input.value.trim();\n            \n            if (!message) return;\n\n            // Clear input\n            input.value = \'\';\n\n            // Add user message\n            addMessage(\'USER\', message, \'user\');\n\n            // Show loading\n            showLoading(true);\n\n            try {\n                // Try to execute as command first\n                if (message.startsWith(\'/\')) {\n                    await executeCommandAPI(message.substring(1));\n                } else {\n                    // Send to LLM for processing\n                    await processWithLLM(message);\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Error:\', error);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Error: ${error.message}`, \'system\');\n            } finally {\n                showLoading(false);\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function processWithLLM(message) {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/llm/generate\', {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        prompt: message,\n                        user_context: {\n                            name: userName,\n                            business_type: businessType,\n                            goal: userGoal\n                        }\n                    })\n                });\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                if (data.text) {\n                    addMessage(\'GENERATED\', data.text, \'generated\');\n                } else {\n                    addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \'Response received but no text generated.\', \'system\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                throw new Error(`LLM processing failed: ${error.message}`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function executeCommandAPI(command) {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/command/execute\', {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        command: command,\n                        args: {}\n                    })\n                });\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                if (data.result) {\n                    addMessage(\'VERIFIED\', JSON.stringify(data.result, null, 2), \'verified\');\n                } else {\n                    addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \'Command executed successfully.\', \'system\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                throw new Error(`Command execution failed: ${error.message}`);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Quick Command Execution\n        async function executeCommand(cmd) {\n            showLoading(true);\n            \n            try {\n                switch(cmd) {\n                    case \'status\':\n                        const statusResp = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/status\');\n                        const statusData = await statusResp.json();\n                        addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Status: ${statusData.status}\\nSystems: ${Object.keys(statusData.systems).length}/21 operational`, \'system\');\n                        break;\n                    \n                    case \'health\':\n                        const healthResp = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/monitoring/health\');\n                        const healthData = await healthResp.json();\n                        addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Health: ${healthData.status}\\nUptime: ${healthData.uptime || \'N/A\'}`, \'system\');\n                        break;\n                    \n                    case \'generate\':\n                        document.getElementById(\'user-input\').value = \'Generate a sample business report\';\n                        handleSubmit();\n                        break;\n                    \n                    case \'help\':\n                        addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \n                            \'Available Commands:\\n\' +\n                            \'- Type naturally to chat with AI\\n\' +\n                            \'- Use /command for direct commands\\n\' +\n                            \'- Click tasks to see details\\n\' +\n                            \'- Use sidebar for quick actions\', \n                            \'system\'\n                        );\n                        break;\n                    \n                    default:\n                        addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Executing: ${cmd}...`, \'system\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Error executing ${cmd}: ${error.message}`, \'system\');\n            } finally {\n                showLoading(false);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Tab Switching\n        function switchTab(tabName) {\n            // Update tab buttons\n            document.querySelectorAll(\'.tab\').forEach(tab => {\n                tab.classList.remove(\'active\');\n            });\n            event.target.classList.add(\'active\');\n\n            // Show appropriate content\n            addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Switched to ${tabName} view`, \'system\');\n        }\n\n        // Modal Functions\n        function openTaskModal(taskId, taskName) {\n            document.getElementById(\'modal-task-title\').textContent = taskName;\n            document.getElementById(\'modal-llm-description\').textContent = \'Loading LLM description...\';\n            document.getElementById(\'modal-system-description\').textContent = \'Loading system Task Detail Modal (NEW FEATURE)\n**Before:**\n```\n❌ Tasks not clickable\n❌ No way to view details\n❌ No LLM/System descriptions\n```\n\n**After:**\n```html\n<!-- Split-screen modal with LLM + System views -->\n<div id="task-modal" class="modal">\n    <div class="modal-content">\n        <div class="modal-body">\n            <!-- LEFT: LLM Description -->\n            <div class="modal-section">\n                <div class="modal-section-title">LLM Description</div>\n                <div class="modal-section-content">\n                    Natural language explanation of what the task does\n                </div>\n            </div>\n            \n            <!-- RIGHT: System Description -->\n            <div class="modal-section">\n                <div class="modal-section-title">System Description</div>\n                <div class="modal-section-content">\n                    Technical details of system process\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n</div>\n```\n\n**Result:** ✅ Click any task → See LLM description (left) + System description (right)\n\n#### 4. Visual Feedback System (NEW FEATURE)\n**Before:**\n```\n❌ No indication of system processing\n❌ Unclear if system received input\n❌ No connection status\n```\n\n**After:**\n```javascript\n// Loading Indicator\n<div id="loading" class="loading">\n    <span class="loading-dots">Processing...</span>\n</div>\n\n// Status Indicator (bottom-right)\n<div id="status-indicator" class="status-indicator">\n    <span id="status-text">Connected</span>\n</div>\n\n// Real-time Socket.IO Updates\nsocket.on(\'connect\', () => {\n    showStatus(\'Connected to Murphy System\', 3000);\n});\n\nsocket.on(\'task_update\', (data) => {\n    addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Task Update: ${data.message}`, \'system\');\n});\n```\n\n**Result:** ✅ Clear visual feedback at all times\n\n#### 5. Backend Communication (FIXED)\n**Before:**\n```\n❌ Using non-existent /api/chat endpoint (404 errors)\n❌ No proper error handling\n❌ Unclear which endpoints to use\n```\n\n**After:**\n```javascript\n// Correct endpoint usage\nasync function processWithLLM(message) {\n    const response = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/llm/generate\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n            prompt: message,\n            user_context: { name, business_type, goal }\n        })\n    });\n    const data = await response.json();\n    addMessage(\'GENERATED\', data.text, \'generated\');\n}\n\nasync function executeCommandAPI(command) {\n    const response = await fetch(\'http://localhost:3002/api/command/execute\', {\n        method: \'POST\',\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ command, args: {} })\n    });\n    const data = await response.json();\n    addMessage(\'VERIFIED\', JSON.stringify(data.result, null, 2), \'verified\');\n}\n```\n\n**Result:** ✅ All endpoints working (6/6 tests passed - 100% success rate)\n\n## Backend Test Results\n\n```\n============================================================\nMURPHY UI BACKEND COMMUNICATION TEST\n============================================================\n\n✅ GET  /api/status              - Command Execution\n✅ POST /api/librarian/ask       - Librarian Knowledge Query\n\nPassed: 6/6\nSuccess Rate: 100.0%\n\n✅ ALL TESTS PASSED - UI Backend Communication Working!\n```\n\n## Feature Comparison\n\n| Feature | Old UI | Fixed UI |\n|---------|--------|----------|\n| Message Separation | ❌ Stacking | ✅ Clean spacing |\n| Scrolling | ❌ None | ✅ Smooth scroll |\n| Task Details | ❌ Not clickable | ✅ Modal with LLM + System views |\n| Loading Indicator | ❌ None | ✅ Animated dots |\n| Status Indicator | ❌ None | ✅ Bottom-right indicator |\n| Socket.IO | ❌ Basic | ✅ Full real-time updates |\n| Backend Communication | ❌ Wrong endpoints | ✅ Correct endpoints |\n| Error Handling | ❌ Minimal | ✅ Comprehensive |\n| Visual Feedback | ❌ None | ✅ Multiple indicators |\n| Custom Scrollbar | ❌ Default | ✅ Styled green theme |\n\n## User Experience Flow\n\n### 1. Reconnecting...\', 0);\n            });\n\n            socket.on(\'task_update\', (data) => {\n                console.log(\'Task update:\', data);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Task Update: ${data.message || JSON.stringify(data)}`, \'system\');\n            });\n\n            socket.on(\'error\', (error) => {\n                console.error(\'Socket error:\', error);\n                addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Error: ${error.message || error}`, \'system\');\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Load Commands\n        function loadCommands() {\n            const listEl = document.getElementById(\'command-list\');\n            commands.forEach(cmd => {\n                const cmdEl = document.createElement(\'div\');\n                cmdEl.className = \'command-item\';\n                cmdEl.innerHTML = `\n                    <div class="command-name">${cmd.name}</div>\n                    <div class="command-desc">${cmd.desc}</div>\n                `;\n                cmdEl.onclick = () => {\n                    document.getElementById(\'user-input\').value = cmd.name;\n                    document.getElementById(\'user-input\').focus();\n                };\n                listEl.appendChild(cmdEl);\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Check Initialization\n        async function checkInitialization() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/status`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                if (!data.initialized) {\n                    showOnboardingStep(0);\n                    document.getElementById(\'onboarding-modal\').classList.add(\'active\');\n                } else {\n                    addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \'Murphy System ready. Type /help for commands or use natural language.\', \'system\');\n                    updateStatus();\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\'Initialization check failed:\', error);\n                showOnboardingStep(0);\n                document.getElementById(\'onboarding-modal\').classList.add(\'active\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Setup Event Listeners\n        function setupEventListeners() {\n            document.getElementById(\'submit-btn\').addEventListener(\'click\', handleSubmit);\n            document.getElementById(\'user-input\').addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n                if (e.key === \'Enter\') handleSubmit();\n            });\n\n            // Tab switching\n            document.querySelectorAll(\'.tab\').forEach(tab => {\n                tab.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n                    document.querySelectorAll(\'.tab\').forEach(t => t.classList.remove(\'active\'));\n                    tab.classList.add(\'active\');\n                    addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', `Switched to ${tab.dataset.tab} view`, \'system\');\n                });\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Onboarding\n        function showOnboardingStep(step) {\n            const stepData = onboardingSteps[step];\n            const textEl =          \n            textEl.textContent = stepData.text;\n            inputsEl.innerHTML = \'\';\n            \n            if (stepData.input) {\n                if (stepData.input.type ===  }\n            }\n            \n            if (stepData.final) {\n                btnEl.textContent = \'Start Using Murphy\';\n                btnEl.onclick = finishOnboarding;\n            } else userData[stepData.input.key] = input.value;\n            }\n            \n            onboardingStep = currentStep + 1;\n            if (onboardingStep < onboardingSteps.length) {\n                showOnboardingStep(onboardingStep);\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function finishOnboarding() {\n            document.getElementById(\'onboarding-modal\').classList.remove(\'active\');\n            \n            addMessage(\'SYSTEM\', \'Initializing Murphy System...\', \'system\');\n            \n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/initialize`, {\n                    method: \'POST\',\n                    headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\' },\n                    body:
